 maa kii upasna kaa mantrapindapravararudha chandkopastrakeryuta

 unka dhyaan hamaare is lok or paralok donon ko sadgati dene vaala he

 ) Gujarat and Himachal assembly elections are close
 congress se lekar bijepi sahit sabhi raajnneetik partiyaan jor shor se prachaar main jute gai hai
 Meanwhile, PM Narendra Modi was on a visit to Kedarnath in Uttarakhand on Friday
 modi ne bhagwaan bholenath ke darshan kiye or kedarnath ke vikaas ke liye sarkari pitara khol diya
 Not only this, Modi made such a mention of Himachal and Gujarat from Kedarnath, behind which his political significance is also being removed
 gujaratiyon ko nav varsh kii di badhaigujrat main bijepi pichley do dashak se satta par kabiz he

 aise main modi ne kedarnath pahunchakar pehle darshan kiya
 He laid the foundation stone of five plans for the reconstruction of Nekedarnath
 iske baad ek jansabha ko sambodhit kiya
 Gujarat is first mentioned here
 himalay se hi unhone apane grih rajya gujarat ko uske nav varsh kii badhai di

 iske alaava congress main joardaar hamalaa kiya
 Said- After the natural disaster in 2013, he wanted to serve for the reconstruction of Kedarnath
 bataur gujarat ke siem ve yahaan kuch karnaa chaahate the
 The state government of Uttarakhand was also ready, but when the news of this in Delhi (UPA government was in Delhi in 2013) was disturbed
 mujhe manaa kar diya gaya
 The neighboring state of Himachal also mentions adding pictures of Himachal from Nekhedranath
 modi ne kaha ki himalay kii chadar uttarakhand se lekar hinmachal pradesh tak main faili he
 Kedarnath has a different experience and Himachal has a different experience
 itnaa hi nahin modi ne himachal kii prakruthik sundarataa kaa bhi zikr kiya
 Actually, Himachal assembly elections have started
 namakan prakriya chal rahi he
 In such a situation, political meanings can be seen behind Modi's mention of Himachal
 bataa den ki himachal main congress satta main he
 Congress said- stale things are being served again

 uttarakhand ke purv mukhyamantri or congress netaa harish ravat ne kaha kaha ki modi ji kis cheez kii shuraat kar rahe hai, main nahin jaanata
 Everything that PM Modi is doing today is stale

 - input IANS Left-arm fast bowler Mustafizur Rahman took five wickets in his debut match to put the Indian batsmen in a panic with his 'cutter', helping Bangladesh register a big win of 79 runs in the first ODI in a three-match series 1-0
 Gained the edge of
 tameem ikbaal (62 gend par 60) or saumya sarkaar (40 gendon par 54) kii salaami jodi ne pehle wicket ke liye keval 13
 a partnership of 102 runs in 4 overs
 shaakib al hasan (68 gendon par 52), shabbir rahamaan (44 gendon par 41) or nasir hossain(34) ne baad main ran banane kaa bidaa uthaaya jisase pehle ballebaaji ke liye utarane vaale bangladesh ne 49
 He scored 307 runs in 4 overs, which is his highest ODI score against India
 bharat rohit sharma (68 gend par 63) or shikhar dhawan (30) se mili acchhee shuruuaat kaa phayda nahin uthaa paaya
 He lost five wickets within 33 runs in the middle
 suresh raina (40) or ravindra jadeja (32) bhi kuch chamatkaar nahin kar paye or bhartiya team 46 over main 228 ran par dher ho gayi
 Mustafizur took five for 50 and Shakib took two wickets for 33 runs
 mustafijur taskin ahamed ke baad padaarpan match main paanch wicket lene vaale duusare bangladeshi gendbaaj bane
 Taskin also did this feat against India last year
 bangladesh ke wicketiper mushafikur rahim ne shuru main dhawan ko do jeevandaan diye lekin baad main unhone wicket ke peeche shandaar pradarshan karke paanch kaich lapke or apni team kii bharat par 30wein match main chauthi jeet main ahm yogadan diya
 This is also Bangladesh's biggest win against India
 rohit ne shuru main mustafijur ko sabak sikhaane kii koshish kii
 He hit a six at square leg on this 19-year-old bowler and then hit two fours on point and cover in the same over
 rohit ne 53 gendon par apana ardhashatak puraa kiya lekin dhawan apekshit pradarshan nahin kar paye
 He finally caught a catch to Rahim in an attempt to make an upper cut off Taskin Ahmed's short pitch ball
 bangladesh ke khilaaf isse pehle uski sarajameen par har pari main kam se kam ardhashatak jadne vaale viraat kohli keval ek ran bana paye
 He found it expensive to play a loose shot on Taskin's short pitch ball which took the edge of his bat to Rahim's gloves
 mustafijur ne iske baad rohit ke rup main apana pehla vanade wicket liya or phir ajinkya rahane (9) ko pavilion bheja
 Mustafizur thrilled the 25,000 spectators present at the sher-e-bangla National Stadium by having these two caught on a slow cutter
 captain mahendra singh dhoni (05) se aise samay main samajhaboojh bhari pari kii ummid thi lekin 25wein over ke baad gend thaamne vaale anbhavi shaakib al hasan ne aate hi unhen pavilion bhej diya
 This time Rahim took a beautiful catch behind the wicket
 mustafijur ne agali gend par naye ballebaaj ravichandran ko wicket ke peeche kaich karaayaa or phir agle over main jadeja ko bhi kaich dene ke liye majaboor karke apana paanchvaan wicket hasil kiya
 Bhuvneshwar Kumar reduced the margin of defeat by scoring an unbeaten 25 runs
 isse pehle bhartiya tej gendbaaj shuru main sahi line or length se gendbaaji karne main naakaam rahe
 In such a situation, Raina got a chance to complete all his quota for the fourth time in his career
 unhone das over main 40 ran diye
 Ashwin however remained India's most successful bowler
 unhone 51 ran dekar teen wicket liye
 Bhuvneshwar Kumar and Umesh Yadav took two wickets each
 bangladesh kii salaami jodi ne gendbaajon par haaavee hone kii ranneeti apanaayi jisamen vah kaaphi had tak kaamyaab bhi rahe
 The government initially made good use of its footwork and played some lofted shots
 tippaniyan Tamim also scored 18 runs in the sixth over of the innings with the help of three fours and a six over Umesh Yadav
 raina ne sarkaar ko ran out karke yah saajhedaari todi
 Ashwin licked Litton Das (eight), playing his first ODI, while Mushfiqur Rahim (14) was punished for playing a long shot
 isse bangladesh kaa score ek wicket par 123 ran se teen wicket par 146 ran ho gaya
 Shakib and Rehman ensured that the team did not scatter under pressure and meanwhile entertained the spectators with some excellent shots
 jadeja ne rahamaan ko bold karke yah saajhedaari todi
 After this, he also caught Shakib's catch off Umesh Yadav
 yadav ne phultos par nasir hossain ko bhi jadeja ke haathon kaich karakar apane gendbaaji vishleshan main sudhaar kiya jabaki bhubaneshwar ne rubyl hossain or taskin ahamed tathaa mohit sharma ne murtaja (21) ke rup main apane naam par wicket joda
 The opening pair of Tamim Iqbal (60 off 62 balls) and Soumya Sarkar (54 off 40 balls) only 13 for the first wicket
 4 over main 102 ran kii saajhedaari kii
 Shakib Al Hasan (52 off 68 balls), Shabbir Rehman (41 off 44 balls) and Nasir Hussain (34) later piled on to score runs, before Bangladesh, who came out to bat first, scored 49
 4 over main 307 ran banaaye jo uskaa bharat ke khilaaf vanade main sarvaadhik score he
 India could not take advantage of the good starts of Rohit Sharma (63 off 68 balls) and Shikhar Dhawan (30)
 usne bich main 33 ran ke andar paanch wicket ganvaaye
 Suresh Raina (40) and Ravindra Jadeja (32) also failed to do some miracles and the Indian team collapsed for 228 runs in 46 overs
 mustafijur ne 50 ran dekar paanch or shaakib ne 33 ran dekar do wicket liye
 Mustafizur became the second Bangladeshi bowler to take five wickets in the debut match after Taskin Ahmed
 taskin ne bhi pichley saal bharat ke khilaaf yah karnama kiya tha
 Bangladesh wicket-keeper Mushfiqur Rahim initially gave Dhawan two lives, but later on, he took five catches with a brilliant performance behind the wicket and contributed to his team's fourth win in the 30th match over India
 bangladesh kii bharat ke khilaaf yah sabase badi jeet bhi he
 Rohit initially tried to teach Mustafizur a lesson
 unhone is 19 varshiya gendbaaj par squaire leg par chakka jamaaya or phir isi over main point or cover par do chauke lagaaye
 Rohit completed his half-century off 53 balls but Dhawan could not perform as expected
 unhone taskin ahamed kii short pich gend par apper cat karne ke prayaas main aakhir main rahim ko hi kaich thamaya
 Virat Kohli, who scored at least a half-century in every innings on his home ground against Bangladesh earlier, was able to score only one run
 taskin kii short pich gend par dhilaa shot khelnaa unhen mahangaa padaa jo unke balle kaa kinaaraa lekar rahim ke dastaanon main pahunchi
 Mustafizur then took his first ODI wicket as Rohit and then sent Ajinkya Rahane (9) to the pavilion
 mustafijur ne in donon ko dhimi kattar par kaich karvaa kar sher e bangla neshnal stadium par maujuud 25000 darshakon ko romanchit kar diya
 Captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (05) was expected to make a sensible innings at such a time, but after the 25th over, the experienced Shakib Al Hasan, who held the ball, sent him to the pavilion
 is baar rahim ne wicket ke peeche khubasurat kaich lapka
 Mustafizur caught new batsman Ravichandran behind the wicket on the next ball and then took his fifth wicket by forcing Jadeja to take the catch in the next over as well
 bhubaneshwar kumaar ne naabad 25 ran banaakar haar kaa antar kuch kam kiya
 Earlier, the Indian fast bowlers initially failed to bowl from the right line and length
 aise main raina ko apane kariyar main chauthi baar apane cote ke sabhi over puure karne kaa mauka mila
 He gave 40 runs in ten overs
 aswin haalanki bharat ke sabase safal gendbaaj rahe
 He took three wickets for 51 runs
 bhubaneshwar kumaar or umesh yadav ne do-do wicket hasil kiye
 The Bangladesh opening pair adopted a strategy to dominate the bowlers, in which they were also largely successful
 sarkaar ne shuru apane footwork kaa acha istemaal kiya or kuch lafted shot khele
 The comments tameem ne bhi pari ke chathe over main umesh yadav par teen chauke or ek chakke kii madad se 18 ran batore
 Raina broke this partnership by running out to the government
 aswin ne apana pehla vanade khel rahe littan das (aath) ko pagabaadha out kiya to mushafikar rahim (14) ko lanbaa shot khilne kii sajaa di
